</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">August&#160;1, 2024 &#8212; Intelligent power management company Eaton Corporation plc (NYSE&#58;ETN) today announced that earnings per share were $2.48 for the second quarter of 2024, a second quarter record and up 33% over the second quarter of 2023. Excluding charges of $0.20 per share related to intangible amortization, $0.03 per share related to a multi-year restructuring program, and $0.02 per share related to acquisitions and divestitures, adjusted earnings per share of $2.73 were a record and up 24% over the second quarter of 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Sales in the quarter were $6.4 billion, a record and up 8% from the second quarter of 2023. Organic sales were up 9%, which was partially offset by 1% from negative currency translation.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Segment margins were 23.7%, a quarterly record and a 210-basis point improvement over the second quarter of 2023. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Operating cash flow was $946 million and free cash flow was $759 million, both second quarter records and up 11% and 10%, respectively, over the same period in 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Craig Arnold, Eaton chairman and chief executive officer, said, &#8220;We continue to see strong demand across our markets &#8211; due to electrification, energy transition and reindustrialization &#8211; resulting in record earnings and continued backlog growth. We&#8217;re making capacity investments in key product lines to support structurally higher growth, and we remain confident in our outlook. As a result, we are increasing our guidance for the year.&#34;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:150%">Guidance</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New raised $100 million and narrowed to between $3.4 billion to $3.6 billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Organic sales were up 3.5%, which was partially offset by 1.5% from negative currency translation. Operating profits were $305 million, a second quarter record and up 5% over the second quarter of 2023. Operating margins in the quarter were 19.0%, a second quarter record and up 50 basis points over the second quarter of 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">The twelve-month rolling average of orders in the second quarter was up 7% organically. Backlog at the end of June was up 16% organically over June 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">On a rolling twelve-month basis, the book-to-bill ratio for the Electrical businesses remained strong at 1.1.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Aerospace segment sales were a record $955 million, up 13% from the second quarter of 2023, driven entirely by organic sales growth. Operating profits were $206 million and operating margins in the quarter were 21.5%.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">The twelve-month rolling average of orders in the second quarter was up 4% organically. The backlog at the end of June was up 14% over June 2023. On a rolling twelve-month basis, the book-to-bill ratio for the Aerospace segment remained strong at 1.1.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">The Vehicle segment posted sales of $723 million, down 4% from the second quarter of 2023, driven by organic sales decline of 3% and negative currency translation of 1%. Operating profits were $130 million, up 13% over the second quarter of 2023. Operating margins in the quarter were 18.0%, up 270 basis points over the second quarter of 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">eMobility segment sales were a record $189 million, up 18% over the second quarter of 2023, driven entirely by organic sales growth. The segment recorded an operating profit of $2 million and operating margins in the quarter were 1.3%.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Eaton is an intelligent power management company dedicated to protecting the environment and improving the quality of life for people everywhere. We make products for the data center, utility, industrial, commercial, machine building, residential, aerospace and mobility markets. We are guided by our commitment to do business right, to operate sustainably and to help our customers manage power &#9472; today and well into the future. By capitalizing on the global growth trends of electrification and digitalization, we&#8217;re accelerating the planet&#8217;s transition to renewable energy sources, helping to solve the world&#8217;s most urgent power management challenges, and building a more sustainable society for people today and generations to come. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Eaton was founded in 1911 and has been listed on the New York Stock Exchange for more than a century. We reported revenues of $23.2 billion in 2023 and serve customers in more than 160 countries. For more information, visit www.eaton.com. These financial measures include adjusted earnings, adjusted earnings per ordinary share, and free cash flow, each of which differs from the most directly comparable measure calculated in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP). A reconciliation of each of these financial measures to the most directly comparable GAAP measure is included in this earnings release. Management believes that these financial measures are useful to investors because they provide additional meaningful financial information that should be considered when assessing our business performance and trends, and they allow investors to more easily compare Eaton Corporation plc's (Eaton or the Company) financial performance period to period. Exertherm is reported within the Electrical Americas business segment.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Acquisition of a 49%</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">stake in NordicEPOD AS</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-indent:13.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On May 31, 2024, Eaton acquired a 49 percent stake in NordicEPOD AS, which designs and assembles standardized power modules for data centers in the Nordic region. Eaton accounts for this investment on the equity method of accounting and it is reported within the Electrical Global business segment.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div id="i20f30811efa14066964c5b3fe0e756e9_25"></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Note 3. These charges were included in Cost of products sold, Selling and administrative expense, Research and development expense, or Other expense (income) - net. In Business Segment Information, the charges were included in Other expense - net.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><div id="i20f30811efa14066964c5b3fe0e756e9_31"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Note 4. RESTRUCTURING CHARGES</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:13.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the second quarter of 2020, Eaton initiated a multi-year restructuring program to reduce its cost structure and gain efficiencies in its business segments and at corporate in order to initially respond to declining market conditions brought on by the COVID-19 pandemic. Since the inception of the program, the Company incurred expenses of $199&#160;million for workforce reductions and $184&#160;million for plant closing and other costs, resulting in total charges of $382&#160;million through December 31, 2023. This multi-year restructuring program was substantially complete at the end of 2023, with final payments expected to be made in 2024.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:13.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">During the first quarter of 2024, Eaton implemented a new multi-year restructuring program to accelerate opportunities to optimize its operations and global support structure. These actions will better align the Company's functions to support anticipated growth and drive greater effectiveness throughout the Company. Restructuring charges incurred under this program were $15&#160;million in the second quarter and $78&#160;million in the first six months of 2024. This restructuring program is expected to be completed in 2026 and is expected to incur additional expenses related to workforce reductions of $208&#160;million and plant closing and other costs of $89&#160;million, resulting in total estimated charges of $375&#160;million for the entire program. The Company expects mature year benefits of $325&#160;million when the multi-year program is fully implemented.  </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-indent:13.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A summary of restructuring program charges is as follows&#58;</font></div><div
